import torch
import torch.nn as nn
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

cpp_source = r"""
#include <torch/extension.h>
torch::Tensor forward_cuda(
    torch::Tensor pair_repr,
    torch::Tensor pair_mask,
    torch::Tensor ln_in_w,
    torch::Tensor ln_in_b,
    torch::Tensor proj_a_w,
    torch::Tensor proj_a_b,
    torch::Tensor gate_a_w,
    torch::Tensor gate_a_b,
    torch::Tensor proj_b_w,
    torch::Tensor proj_b_b,
    torch::Tensor gate_b_w,
    torch::Tensor gate_b_b,
    torch::Tensor ln_out_w,
    torch::Tensor ln_out_b,
    torch::Tensor out_proj_w,
    torch::Tensor out_proj_b,
    torch::Tensor out_gate_w,
    torch::Tensor out_gate_b
);
"""

cuda_source = r"""
#include <torch/extension.h>
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <ATen/cuda/CUDAContext.h>

constexpr int N = 32;
constexpr int C = 64;
constexpr int H = 32;
constexpr float EPS = 1e-5f;

__device__ __forceinline__ float sigmoidf_fast(float x) {
    return 1.0f / (1.0f + expf(-x));
}

__inline__ __device__ float warp_reduce_sum(float val) {
    #pragma unroll
    for (int offset = 16; offset > 0; offset /= 2) {
        val += __shfl_xor_sync(0xffffffff, val, offset);
    }
    return val;
}

__global__ void fused_forward_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ pair_repr,
    const float* __restrict__ pair_mask,
    const float* __restrict__ ln_in_w,
    const float* __restrict__ ln_in_b,
    const float* __restrict__ proj_a_w,
    const float* __restrict__ proj_a_b,
    const float* __restrict__ gate_a_w,
    const float* __restrict__ gate_a_b,
    const float* __restrict__ proj_b_w,
    const float* __restrict__ proj_b_b,
    const float* __restrict__ gate_b_w,
    const float* __restrict__ gate_b_b,
    const float* __restrict__ ln_out_w,
    const float* __restrict__ ln_out_b,
    const float* __restrict__ out_proj_w,
    const float* __restrict__ out_proj_b,
    const float* __restrict__ out_gate_w,
    const float* __restrict__ out_gate_b,
    float* __restrict__ output,
    int B)
{
    int b = blockIdx.z;
    int i = blockIdx.y;
    int j = blockIdx.x;
    int h = threadIdx.x;
    if (b >= B) return;

    const int stride_repr = N * N * C;
    const int stride_mask = N * N;
    const int base_ij = b * stride_repr + i * N * C + j * C;

    extern __shared__ float smem[];
    float* smem_x_i   = smem;
    float* smem_x_j   = smem + C;
    float* smem_gate  = smem + 2 * C;

    float acc = 0.0f;

    for (int k = 0; k < N; ++k) {
        int base_i = b * stride_repr + i * N * C + k * C;
        int base_j = b * stride_repr + j * N * C + k * C;

        smem_x_i[h]     = pair_repr[base_i + h];
        smem_x_i[h + 32] = pair_repr[base_i + h + 32];
        smem_x_j[h]     = pair_repr[base_j + h];
        smem_x_j[h + 32] = pair_repr[base_j + h + 32];

        float v0 = smem_x_i[h];
        float v1 = smem_x_i[h + 32];
        float sum = v0 + v1;
        sum = warp_reduce_sum(sum);
        float mean = sum * (1.0f / (float)C);
        float d0 = v0 - mean;
        float d1 = v1 - mean;
        float sq = d0 * d0 + d1 * d1;
        sq = warp_reduce_sum(sq);
        float var = sq * (1.0f / (float)C);
        float inv_std = rsqrtf(var + EPS);
        smem_x_i[h]     = d0 * inv_std * ln_in_w[h]     + ln_in_b[h];
        smem_x_i[h + 32] = d1 * inv_std * ln_in_w[h + 32] + ln_in_b[h + 32];

        v0 = smem_x_j[h];
        v1 = smem_x_j[h + 32];
        sum = v0 + v1;
        sum = warp_reduce_sum(sum);
        mean = sum * (1.0f / (float)C);
        d0 = v0 - mean;
        d1 = v1 - mean;
        sq = d0 * d0 + d1 * d1;
        sq = warp_reduce_sum(sq);
        var = sq * (1.0f / (float)C);
        inv_std = rsqrtf(var + EPS);
        smem_x_j[h]     = d0 * inv_std * ln_in_w[h]     + ln_in_b[h];
        smem_x_j[h + 32] = d1 * inv_std * ln_in_w[h + 32] + ln_in_b[h + 32];

        float mask_i = pair_mask[b * stride_mask + i * N + k];
        float mask_j = pair_mask[b * stride_mask + j * N + k];

        float dot_a = 0.0f;
        float dot_ga = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll 8
        for (int c = 0; c < C; ++c) {
            float xv = smem_x_i[c];
            dot_a  += xv * proj_a_w[c * H + h];
            dot_ga += xv * gate_a_w[c * H + h];
        }
        float a_val = (dot_a + proj_a_b[h]) *
                      sigmoidf_fast(dot_ga + gate_a_b[h]) *
                      mask_i;

        float dot_b = 0.0f;
        float dot_gb = 0.0f;
        #pragma unroll 8
        for (int c = 0; c < C; ++c) {
            float xv = smem_x_j[c];
            dot_b  += xv * proj_b_w[c * H + h];
            dot_gb += xv * gate_b_w[c * H + h];
        }
        float b_val = (dot_b + proj_b_b[h]) *
                      sigmoidf_fast(dot_gb + gate_b_b[h]) *
                      mask_j;

        acc += a_val * b_val;
    }

    float sum_out = warp_reduce_sum(acc);
    float mean_out = sum_out * (1.0f / (float)H);
    float diff_out = acc - mean_out;
    float sq_out = diff_out * diff_out;
    sq_out = warp_reduce_sum(sq_out);
    float var_out = sq_out * (1.0f / (float)H);
    acc = diff_out * rsqrtf(var_out + EPS) * ln_out_w[h] + ln_out_b[h];

    smem_gate[h]     = pair_repr[base_ij + h];
    smem_gate[h + 32] = pair_repr[base_ij + h + 32];

    float gate0 = 0.0f;
    float gate1 = 0.0f;
    #pragma unroll 8
    for (int c = 0; c < C; ++c) {
        float xv = smem_gate[c];
        gate0 += xv * out_gate_w[c * C + h];
        gate1 += xv * out_gate_w[c * C + h + 32];
    }
    smem_gate[h]     = sigmoidf_fast(gate0 + out_gate_b[h]);
    smem_gate[h + 32] = sigmoidf_fast(gate1 + out_gate_b[h + 32]);

    smem_x_i[h] = acc;

    for (int c = 0; c < C; ++c) {
        float prod = smem_x_i[h] * out_proj_w[c * H + h];
        prod = warp_reduce_sum(prod);
        if (h == 0) {
            float out_val = prod + out_proj_b[c];
            out_val *= smem_gate[c];
            output[base_ij + c] = out_val;
        }
    }
}

torch::Tensor forward_cuda(
    torch::Tensor pair_repr,
    torch::Tensor pair_mask,
    torch::Tensor ln_in_w,
    torch::Tensor ln_in_b,
    torch::Tensor proj_a_w,
    torch::Tensor proj_a_b,
    torch::Tensor gate_a_w,
    torch::Tensor gate_a_b,
    torch::Tensor proj_b_w,
    torch::Tensor proj_b_b,
    torch::Tensor gate_b_w,
    torch::Tensor gate_b_b,
    torch::Tensor ln_out_w,
    torch::Tensor ln_out_b,
    torch::Tensor out_proj_w,
    torch::Tensor out_proj_b,
    torch::Tensor out_gate_w,
    torch::Tensor out_gate_b)
{
    auto repr = pair_repr.contiguous().to(torch::kFloat32);
    auto mask = pair_mask.contiguous().to(torch::kFloat32);

    int B = repr.size(0);
    auto output = torch::empty_like(repr);

    dim3 grid(N, N, B);
    dim3 block(H);
    size_t smem_size = 3 * C * sizeof(float);

    fused_forward_kernel<<<grid, block, smem_size, at::cuda::getCurrentCUDAStream()>>>(
        repr.data_ptr<float>(),
        mask.data_ptr<float>(),
        ln_in_w.data_ptr<float>(),
        ln_in_b.data_ptr<float>(),
        proj_a_w.data_ptr<float>(),
        proj_a_b.data_ptr<float>(),
        gate_a_w.data_ptr<float>(),
        gate_a_b.data_ptr<float>(),
        proj_b_w.data_ptr<float>(),
        proj_b_b.data_ptr<float>(),
        gate_b_w.data_ptr<float>(),
        gate_b_b.data_ptr<float>(),
        ln_out_w.data_ptr<float>(),
        ln_out_b.data_ptr<float>(),
        out_proj_w.data_ptr<float>(),
        out_proj_b.data_ptr<float>(),
        out_gate_w.data_ptr<float>(),
        out_gate_b.data_ptr<float>(),
        output.data_ptr<float>(),
        B
    );

    return output;
}
"""

_custom_op = load_inline(
    name="fused_tri_mul_outgoing_v3",
    cpp_sources=cpp_source,
    cuda_sources=cuda_source,
    functions=["forward_cuda"],
    extra_cuda_cflags=["-O3", "--use_fast_math"],
    extra_cflags=["-O3"],
    extra_ldflags=["-static-libstdc++"],
    verbose=False,
)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, pair_dim, hidden_dim):
        super().__init__()
        self.layer_norm_in = nn.LayerNorm(pair_dim)
        self.proj_a = nn.Linear(pair_dim, hidden_dim)
        self.gate_a = nn.Linear(pair_dim, hidden_dim)
        self.proj_b = nn.Linear(pair_dim, hidden_dim)
        self.gate_b = nn.Linear(pair_dim, hidden_dim)
        self.layer_norm_out = nn.LayerNorm(hidden_dim)
        self.out_proj = nn.Linear(hidden_dim, pair_dim)
        self.out_gate = nn.Linear(pair_dim, pair_dim)

    def forward(self, pair_repr: torch.Tensor, pair_mask: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
        ln_in_w = self.layer_norm_in.weight
        ln_in_b = self.layer_norm_in.bias
        proj_a_w = self.proj_a.weight.t().contiguous()
        proj_a_b = self.proj_a.bias
        gate_a_w = self.gate_a.weight.t().contiguous()
        gate_a_b = self.gate_a.bias
        proj_b_w = self.proj_b.weight.t().contiguous()
        proj_b_b = self.proj_b.bias
        gate_b_w = self.gate_b.weight.t().contiguous()
        gate_b_b = self.gate_b.bias
        ln_out_w = self.layer_norm_out.weight
        ln_out_b = self.layer_norm_out.bias
        out_proj_w = self.out_proj.weight
        out_proj_b = self.out_proj.bias
        out_gate_w = self.out_gate.weight.t().contiguous()
        out_gate_b = self.out_gate.bias

        return _custom_op.forward_cuda(
            pair_repr, pair_mask,
            ln_in_w, ln_in_b,
            proj_a_w, proj_a_b,
            gate_a_w, gate_a_b,
            proj_b_w, proj_b_b,
            gate_b_w, gate_b_b,
            ln_out_w, ln_out_b,
            out_proj_w, out_proj_b,
            out_gate_w, out_gate_b,
        )
